import React, { useState, useContext } from "react"; 
import { Link, useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import { UserContext } from "../context/UserContext";
import { GoogleLogin } from "@react-oauth/google";
import "./Auth.css";

export default function LoginPage() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [email, setEmail] = useState("");
  const [password, setPassword] = useState("");
  const [errorMsg, setErrorMsg] = useState("");
  const [successMsg, setSuccessMsg] = useState(""); 
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);
  const { login } = useContext(UserContext);

  const handleLogin = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setErrorMsg(""); setSuccessMsg(""); setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      const response = await fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Auth/login", {
        method: "POST", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ email, password }),
      });
      const data = await response.json();
      if (response.ok) {
        // âš¡ LÆ¯U TOÃ€N Bá»˜ 5 TRÆ¯á»œNG Dá»® LIá»†U Tá»ª API
        login({ 
          token: data.token, 
          userId: data.userId, 
          email: data.email, 
          fullName: data.fullName, 
          role: data.role 
        });
        setSuccessMsg(`ÄÄƒng nháº­p thÃ nh cÃ´ng! Xin chÃ o ${data.fullName}`);
        setTimeout(() => navigate("/"), 2000);
      } else { 
        setErrorMsg(data.message || "Sai tÃ i khoáº£n hoáº·c máº­t kháº©u!"); 
      }
    } catch (error) { 
      setErrorMsg("KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ káº¿t ná»‘i Ä‘áº¿n Server."); 
    } finally { 
      setIsLoading(false); 
    }
  };

  const handleGoogleSuccess = async (credentialResponse) => {
    setIsLoading(true); setErrorMsg(""); setSuccessMsg(""); 
    try {
      const response = await fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Auth/google", {
        method: "POST", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ idToken: credentialResponse.credential }),
      });
      const data = await response.json();
      if (response.ok) {
        // âš¡ LÆ¯U TOÃ€N Bá»˜ 5 TRÆ¯á»œNG Dá»® LIá»†U Tá»ª API (GOOGLE AUTH)
        login({ 
          token: data.token, 
          userId: data.userId, 
          email: data.email, 
          fullName: data.fullName, 
          role: data.role 
        });
        setSuccessMsg(`ÄÄƒng nháº­p Google thÃ nh cÃ´ng!`);
        setTimeout(() => navigate("/"), 2000);
      } else { 
        setErrorMsg("XÃ¡c thá»±c Google tháº¥t báº¡i!"); 
      }
    } catch (error) { 
      setErrorMsg("Lá»—i káº¿t ná»‘i API Google."); 
    } finally { 
      setIsLoading(false); 
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="auth-container">
      <h2 className="auth-title">ÄÄƒng Nháº­p</h2>
      
      {errorMsg && <div className="auth-msg error">{errorMsg}</div>}
      {successMsg && <div className="auth-msg success">{successMsg}</div>}

      <form onSubmit={handleLogin} className="auth-form">
        <div className="form-group">
          <label>Email:</label>
          <input type="email" value={email} onChange={(e) => setEmail(e.target.value)} required placeholder="Nháº­p email cá»§a báº¡n" />
        </div>
        <div className="form-group">
          <label>Máº­t kháº©u:</label>
          <input type="password" value={password} onChange={(e) => setPassword(e.target.value)} required placeholder="Nháº­p máº­t kháº©u" />
        </div>
        <button type="submit" disabled={isLoading} className="btn-submit"> 
          {isLoading ? "Äang xá»­ lÃ½..." : "ÄÄƒng Nháº­p"}
        </button>
      </form>
      
      <div className="auth-divider">
        <div className="line"></div><span className="text">HOáº¶C</span><div className="line"></div>
      </div>

      <div className="auth-google-btn">
        <GoogleLogin onSuccess={handleGoogleSuccess} onError={() => setErrorMsg("ÄÄƒng nháº­p Google tháº¥t báº¡i")} shape="pill" theme="outline" />
      </div>

      <div className="auth-footer">
        ChÆ°a cÃ³ tÃ i khoáº£n? <Link to="/register" className="auth-link">ÄÄƒng kÃ½ ngay</Link>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState, useEffect, useMemo } from "react";
import { useSearchParams } from "react-router-dom"; 
import "./MainPage.css";
import ProductCard from "../components/product/ProductCard";

// 1. Import áº£nh banner tá»« thÆ° má»¥c assets
import bannerImg from "../assets/bn.jpg"; 

export default function MainPage() {
  const [searchParams] = useSearchParams();
  const searchQuery = searchParams.get("search") || "";
  const [products, setProducts] = useState([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState("");

  const [selectedShapes, setSelectedShapes] = useState([]);
  const [selectedMaterials, setSelectedMaterials] = useState([]);
  const [selectedPrice, setSelectedPrice] = useState("all"); 

  const [currentPage, setCurrentPage] = useState(1);
  const productsPerPage = 12;

  useEffect(() => { 
    const fetchProducts = async () => { 
      setIsLoading(true); 
      setError(""); 
      try { 
        const response = await fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Frames?page=1&pageSize=100"); 
        if (response.ok) { 
          const data = await response.json(); 
          const allFrames = data.items || data || [];

          
          const uniqueFrames = [];
          const seenNames = new Set();
          
          allFrames.forEach(frame => {
            if (!seenNames.has(frame.frameName)) {
              seenNames.add(frame.frameName);
              uniqueFrames.push(frame); 
            }
          });
          
          setProducts(uniqueFrames); 
        } else { 
          setError("KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ táº£i danh sÃ¡ch sáº£n pháº©m."); 
        } 
      } catch (err) { 
        setError("Lá»—i káº¿t ná»‘i Ä‘áº¿n mÃ¡y chá»§ Backend."); 
      } finally { 
        setIsLoading(false); 
      } 
    }; 
    fetchProducts(); 
  }, []);

  const filteredProducts = useMemo(() => {
    return products.filter((product) => {
      const productName = product.frameName || product.name || "";
      const searchMatch = productName.toLowerCase().includes(searchQuery.toLowerCase());

      const productShape = product.shape || "";
      const productMaterial = product.material || "";

      const shapeMatch = selectedShapes.length === 0 || selectedShapes.includes(productShape);
      const materialMatch = selectedMaterials.length === 0 || selectedMaterials.includes(productMaterial);

      const price = product.basePrice || product.price || 0;
      let priceMatch = true;
      if (selectedPrice === "under15") priceMatch = price < 15;
      else if (selectedPrice === "15to20") priceMatch = price >= 15 && price <= 20;
      else if (selectedPrice === "over20") priceMatch = price > 20;

      return searchMatch && shapeMatch && materialMatch && priceMatch;
    });
  }, [products, selectedShapes, selectedMaterials, selectedPrice, searchQuery]);

  useEffect(() => { setCurrentPage(1); }, [selectedShapes, selectedMaterials, selectedPrice, searchQuery]);
  useEffect(() => { window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: "smooth" }); }, [currentPage]);

  const indexOfLastProduct = currentPage * productsPerPage;
  const indexOfFirstProduct = indexOfLastProduct - productsPerPage;
  const currentProducts = filteredProducts.slice(indexOfFirstProduct, indexOfLastProduct);
  const totalPages = Math.ceil(filteredProducts.length / productsPerPage);

  const paginate = (pageNumber) => setCurrentPage(pageNumber);
  const nextPage = () => setCurrentPage((prev) => (prev < totalPages ? prev + 1 : prev));
  const prevPage = () => setCurrentPage((prev) => (prev > 1 ? prev - 1 : prev));

  const handleCheckboxChange = (setState, state, value) => {
    if (state.includes(value)) setState(state.filter((item) => item !== value));
    else setState([...state, value]);
  };

  return (
    <div className="main-page">
      
      
      <div style={{ width: '100%', marginLeft: '40px', overflow: 'hidden' }}>
        <img 
          src={bannerImg} 
          alt="Khuyáº¿n mÃ£i FGlasses" 
          style={{ width: '100%', height: 'auto', display: 'block', objectFit: 'cover' }} 
        />
      </div>

      <div className="main-header">
        <h1>KhÃ¡m phÃ¡ bá»™ sÆ°u táº­p kÃ­nh</h1>
          
        
        {searchQuery && (
          <p style={{ marginTop: '10px', fontSize: '18px', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>
            Káº¿t quáº£ tÃ¬m kiáº¿m cho: "<span style={{color: '#0070c9'}}>{searchQuery}</span>"
          </p>
        )}
      </div>

      <div className="main-content">
        
        <aside className="sidebar-filter">
          <h3>Bá»™ lá»c sáº£n pháº©m</h3>
          <div className="filter-group">
            <h4>HÃ¬nh dÃ¡ng gá»ng</h4>
            <label className="filter-label"><input type="checkbox" checked={selectedShapes.includes("Rectangle")} onChange={() => handleCheckboxChange(setSelectedShapes, selectedShapes, "Rectangle")} /> Chá»¯ nháº­t (Rectangle)</label>
            <label className="filter-label"><input type="checkbox" checked={selectedShapes.includes("Square")} onChange={() => handleCheckboxChange(setSelectedShapes, selectedShapes, "Square")} /> VuÃ´ng (Square)</label>
            <label className="filter-label"><input type="checkbox" checked={selectedShapes.includes("Round")} onChange={() => handleCheckboxChange(setSelectedShapes, selectedShapes, "Round")} /> TrÃ²n (Round)</label>
          </div>
          <div className="filter-group">
            <h4>Cháº¥t liá»‡u</h4>
            <label className="filter-label"><input type="checkbox" checked={selectedMaterials.includes("Plastic")} onChange={() => handleCheckboxChange(setSelectedMaterials, selectedMaterials, "Plastic")} /> Nhá»±a (Plastic)</label>
            <label className="filter-label"><input type="checkbox" checked={selectedMaterials.includes("Stainless Steel")} onChange={() => handleCheckboxChange(setSelectedMaterials, selectedMaterials, "Stainless Steel")} /> ThÃ©p khÃ´ng gá»‰</label>
          </div>
          <div className="filter-group">
            <h4>Má»©c giÃ¡</h4>
            <label className="filter-label"><input type="radio" name="price" checked={selectedPrice === "all"} onChange={() => setSelectedPrice("all")} /> Táº¥t cáº£</label>
            <label className="filter-label"><input type="radio" name="price" checked={selectedPrice === "under15"} onChange={() => setSelectedPrice("under15")} /> DÆ°á»›i $15</label>
            <label className="filter-label"><input type="radio" name="price" checked={selectedPrice === "15to20"} onChange={() => setSelectedPrice("15to20")} /> Tá»« $15 - $20</label>
            <label className="filter-label"><input type="radio" name="price" checked={selectedPrice === "over20"} onChange={() => setSelectedPrice("over20")} /> TrÃªn $20</label>
          </div>
        </aside>

        <section className="product-section">
          {isLoading && <p style={{ textAlign: "center", fontSize: "18px", marginTop: "40px" }}>â³ Äang táº£i dá»¯ liá»‡u tá»« mÃ¡y chá»§...</p>}
          {error && <p style={{ textAlign: "center", fontSize: "18px", marginTop: "40px", color: "red" }}>âŒ {error}</p>}

          {!isLoading && !error && filteredProducts.length === 0 ? (
            <p style={{ textAlign: "center", fontSize: "18px", marginTop: "40px", color: "#666" }}>KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y sáº£n pháº©m nÃ o phÃ¹ há»£p.</p>
          ) : (
            <>
              <div className="product-grid">
                {currentProducts.map((product) => (
                  <ProductCard key={product.id || product.frameId} product={product} />
                ))}
              </div>

              {totalPages > 0 && (
                <div className="pagination">
                  <button className="page-btn" onClick={prevPage} disabled={currentPage === 1} style={{ opacity: currentPage === 1 ? 0.5 : 1 }}>TrÆ°á»›c</button>
                  {[...Array(totalPages)].map((_, index) => (
                    <button key={index + 1} className={`page-btn ${currentPage === index + 1 ? "active" : ""}`} onClick={() => paginate(index + 1)}>{index + 1}</button>
                  ))}
                  <button className="page-btn" onClick={nextPage} disabled={currentPage === totalPages} style={{ opacity: currentPage === totalPages ? 0.5 : 1 }}>Sau</button>
                </div>
              )}
            </>
          )}
        </section>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState, useEffect, useContext } from "react";
import { useParams, Link, useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import { UserContext } from "../context/UserContext";
import "./OrderDetail.css";

export default function OrderDetail() {
  const { id } = useParams();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { user } = useContext(UserContext);
  const [order, setOrder] = useState(null);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState("");

  useEffect(() => {
    const token = user?.token || JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("user"))?.token;
    if (!token) { navigate("/login"); return; }

    const fetchOrderDetail = async () => {
      try {
        const res = await fetch(`https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Orders/${id}`, {
          headers: {
            "Content-Type": "application/json",
            Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
          },
        });
        if (res.ok) {
          const data = await res.json();
          setOrder(data);
        } else if (res.status === 404) {
          setError("KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng nÃ y.");
        } else {
          setError(`Lá»—i ${res.status} khi táº£i chi tiáº¿t Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng.`);
        }
      } catch {
        setError("Lá»—i káº¿t ná»‘i. Vui lÃ²ng thá»­ láº¡i.");
      } finally {
        setIsLoading(false);
      }
    };

    fetchOrderDetail();
  }, [id, user, navigate]);

  if (isLoading)
    return <div style={{ textAlign: "center", padding: "60px", color: "#666" }}>â³ Äang táº£i chi tiáº¿t Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng...</div>;

  if (error || !order)
    return (
      <div style={{ textAlign: "center", padding: "60px" }}>
        <h2 style={{ color: "#dc2626" }}>{error || "KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng"}</h2>
        <Link to="/orders" style={{ color: "#3b82f6" }}>â† Quay láº¡i lá»‹ch sá»­ mua hÃ ng</Link>
      </div>
    );

  // âš¡ HÃ€M FORMAT TIá»€N Tá»† Äá»’NG Bá»˜ Y Há»†T CHECKOUT SUCCESS
  const EXCHANGE_RATE = 25400;
  const formatPrice = (n) => {
    const usd = new Intl.NumberFormat("en-US", { 
      style: "currency", 
      currency: "USD", 
      minimumFractionDigits: 0, 
      maximumFractionDigits: 0 
    }).format(n || 0);
    const vnd = new Intl.NumberFormat("vi-VN").format((n || 0) * EXCHANGE_RATE);
    return `${usd}(${vnd} VND)`;
  };

  const getStatusBadge = (status) => {
    const s = status?.toLowerCase() || "";
    const map = {
      pending:    { text: "Chá» xÃ¡c nháº­n",   color: "#d97706", bg: "#fef3c7" },
      confirmed:  { text: "ÄÃ£ xÃ¡c nháº­n",    color: "#059669", bg: "#d1fae5" },
      processing: { text: "Äang xá»­ lÃ½",     color: "#4338ca", bg: "#ede9fe" },
      shipped:    { text: "Äang giao hÃ ng", color: "#7e22ce", bg: "#f3e8ff" },
      delivering: { text: "Äang giao hÃ ng", color: "#7e22ce", bg: "#f3e8ff" },
      delivered:  { text: "HoÃ n thÃ nh",     color: "#059669", bg: "#d1fae5" },
      completed:  { text: "HoÃ n thÃ nh",     color: "#059669", bg: "#d1fae5" },
      cancelled:  { text: "ÄÃ£ huá»·",         color: "#dc2626", bg: "#fee2e2" },
    };
    const s2 = map[s] || { text: status || "KhÃ´ng rÃµ", color: "#6b7280", bg: "#f3f4f6" };
    return (
      <span style={{ fontWeight: "bold", color: s2.color, backgroundColor: s2.bg, padding: "4px 14px", borderRadius: "20px", fontSize: "14px" }}>
        {s2.text}
      </span>
    );
  };

  let receiverName    = (order.user?.fullName || "â€”").replace("Nh?t", "Nháº­t");
  let receiverPhone   = order.user?.phone     || "â€”";
  let receiverEmail   = order.user?.email     || "â€”";
  let shippingAddress = order.shippingAddress || "â€”";
  const orderNote     = order.note            || "KhÃ´ng cÃ³";

  // 2. âš¡ TRICK: BÃ³c tÃ¡ch vá»›i nhiá»u ká»‹ch báº£n (Fallback)
  // Ká»‹ch báº£n 1: Chuáº©n má»›i nháº¥t [TÃªn - SÄT - Email] Äá»‹a chá»‰
  const matchNew = shippingAddress.match(/^\[(.*?) - (.*?) - (.*?)\] (.*)$/);
  // Ká»‹ch báº£n 2: Bá»‹ lá»—i dÆ° ngoáº·c [TÃªn - SÄT] Email] Äá»‹a chá»‰ (nhÆ° trong áº£nh cá»§a báº¡n)
  const matchError = shippingAddress.match(/^\[(.*?) - (.*?)\] (.*?)] (.*)$/);
  // Ká»‹ch báº£n 3: Chuáº©n cÅ© ngÃ y xÆ°a [TÃªn - SÄT] Äá»‹a chá»‰
  const matchOld = shippingAddress.match(/^\[(.*?) - (.*?)\] (.*)$/);

  if (matchNew) {
    receiverName    = matchNew[1];
    receiverPhone   = matchNew[2];
    receiverEmail   = matchNew[3];
    shippingAddress = matchNew[4];
  } else if (matchError) {
    receiverName    = matchError[1];
    receiverPhone   = matchError[2];
    receiverEmail   = matchError[3].trim();
    shippingAddress = matchError[4];
  } else if (matchOld) {
    receiverName    = matchOld[1];
    receiverPhone   = matchOld[2];
    shippingAddress = matchOld[3];
  }

  const itemsList = order.items || order.orderItems || [];

  return (
    <div style={{ maxWidth: "860px", margin: "40px auto", padding: "20px", fontFamily: "sans-serif" }}>
      <Link to="/orders" style={{ color: "#6b7280", textDecoration: "none", fontSize: "14px", display: "inline-block", marginBottom: "20px" }}>
        â† Lá»‹ch sá»­ mua hÃ ng
      </Link>

      <div style={{ backgroundColor: "white", padding: "30px", borderRadius: "12px", boxShadow: "0 2px 12px rgba(0,0,0,0.07)" }}>

        {/* Header */}
        <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", alignItems: "flex-start", borderBottom: "2px solid #f3f4f6", paddingBottom: "18px", marginBottom: "24px", flexWrap: "wrap", gap: "10px" }}>
          <div>
            <h2 style={{ margin: 0, fontSize: "22px" }}>Chi Tiáº¿t ÄÆ¡n HÃ ng</h2>
            <p style={{ margin: "6px 0 0", color: "#6b7280", fontSize: "14px" }}>
              MÃ£ Ä‘Æ¡n: <b style={{ color: "#111827" }}>#{order.orderId}</b>
            </p>
          </div>
          {getStatusBadge(order.status)}
        </div>

        {/* 2 cá»™t thÃ´ng tin */}
        <div style={{ display: "grid", gridTemplateColumns: "1fr 1fr", gap: "16px", marginBottom: "28px" }}>

          {/* ThÃ´ng tin Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng */}
          <div style={{ backgroundColor: "#f9fafb", padding: "18px", borderRadius: "10px", border: "1px solid #e5e7eb" }}>
            <h4 style={{ marginTop: 0, marginBottom: "12px", color: "#374151", fontSize: "15px", borderBottom: "1px solid #e5e7eb", paddingBottom: "8px" }}>
              ThÃ´ng tin Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng
            </h4>
            <p style={{ margin: "6px 0", fontSize: "14px" }}>
              <b>NgÃ y Ä‘áº·t:</b>{" "}
              {order.createdAt ? new Date(order.createdAt).toLocaleString("vi-VN") : "â€”"}
            </p>
            {order.arrivalDate && (
              <p style={{ margin: "6px 0", fontSize: "14px" }}>
                <b>NgÃ y nháº­n hÃ ng:</b> {new Date(order.arrivalDate).toLocaleString("vi-VN")}
              </p>
            )}
            
            <p style={{ margin: "6px 0", fontSize: "14px" }}>
              <b>Ghi chÃº:</b> {orderNote}
            </p>
          </div>

          {/* ThÃ´ng tin giao hÃ ng */}
          <div style={{ backgroundColor: "#f0fdf4", padding: "18px", borderRadius: "10px", border: "1px solid #bbf7d0" }}>
            <h4 style={{ marginTop: 0, marginBottom: "12px", color: "#374151", fontSize: "15px", borderBottom: "1px solid #bbf7d0", paddingBottom: "8px" }}>
              ThÃ´ng tin giao hÃ ng
            </h4>
            <p style={{ margin: "6px 0", fontSize: "14px" }}>
              <b>NgÆ°á»i nháº­n:</b> {receiverName}
            </p>
            <p style={{ margin: "6px 0", fontSize: "14px" }}>
              <b>Sá»‘ Ä‘iá»‡n thoáº¡i:</b> {receiverPhone}
            </p>
            {/* âš¡ THÃŠM DÃ’NG NÃ€Y Äá»‚ HIá»‚N THá»Š EMAIL */}
            {receiverEmail !== "â€”" && (
              <p style={{ margin: "6px 0", fontSize: "14px" }}>
                <b>Email:</b> {receiverEmail}
              </p>
            )}
            <p style={{ margin: "6px 0", fontSize: "14px" }}>
              <b>Äá»‹a chá»‰ giao hÃ ng:</b> {shippingAddress}
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Danh sÃ¡ch sáº£n pháº©m */}
        <h3 style={{ borderBottom: "1px solid #f3f4f6", paddingBottom: "10px", marginBottom: "16px", fontSize: "17px" }}>
          Sáº£n pháº©m Ä‘Ã£ mua
        </h3>

        {itemsList.length === 0 ? (
          <p style={{ textAlign: "center", color: "#9ca3af", fontStyle: "italic", padding: "20px 0" }}>
            KhÃ´ng cÃ³ thÃ´ng tin sáº£n pháº©m.
          </p>
        ) : (
          <div style={{ marginBottom: "24px" }}>
            {itemsList.map((item, index) => {
              const frameName   = item.frame?.frameName || "Gá»ng kÃ­nh";
              const frameColor  = item.selectedColor    || item.frame?.color || null;
              const qty         = item.quantity         || 1;
              const prescriptionUrl = item.prescription?.imageUrl || null;
              
              // âš¡ Cáº¬P NHáº¬T TÃŠN BIáº¾N ÄÃšNG THEO PRODUCT DETAIL (lensSpecification, featureSpecification)
              const lensType    = item.lensType?.lensSpecification || null;
              
              // Support cáº£ 2 trÆ°á»ng há»£p tÃªn object API tráº£ vá»: lensFeature hoáº·c feature
              const lensFeatureObj = item.lensFeature || item.feature;
              const lensFeature = lensFeatureObj?.featureSpecification || null;
              
              // âš¡ BÃ“C TÃCH GIÃ TIá»€N Tá»ª BACKEND (Sá»­ dá»¥ng extraPrice cho tÃ­nh nÄƒng trÃ²ng)
              const framePrice = item.frame?.basePrice || 0;
              const typePrice = item.lensType?.basePrice || 0;
              const featurePrice = lensFeatureObj?.extraPrice || 0;
              const totalLensPrice = typePrice + featurePrice; 

              // âš¡ Tá»± tÃ­nh giÃ¡ Ä‘Æ¡n vá»‹
              const unitPrice = item.orderPrice || item.unitPrice || item.price || (framePrice + totalLensPrice);
              const calculatedFramePrice = framePrice > 0 ? framePrice : (unitPrice - totalLensPrice);

              return (
                <div
                  key={item.orderItemId || index}
                  style={{ display: "flex", flexDirection: "column", padding: "16px 0", borderBottom: "1px dashed #e5e7eb", gap: "12px" }}
                >
                  {/* HÃ€NG 1: TÃŠN Gá»ŒNG KÃNH + GIÃ Gá»ŒNG */}
                  <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", alignItems: "flex-start", width: "100%" }}>
                    <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                      <p style={{ margin: "0 0 4px 0", fontWeight: "bold", fontSize: "16px" }}>
                        {frameName} {frameColor && <span style={{fontSize: "13px", color: "#6b7280", fontWeight: "normal"}}>- MÃ u: {frameColor}</span>}
                      </p>
                      <p style={{ margin: "4px 0 0", fontSize: "13px", color: "#374151" }}>
                        Sá»‘ lÆ°á»£ng: <b>x{qty}</b>
                      </p>
                    </div>
                    {/* GIÃ Gá»ŒNG KÃNH */}
                    <div style={{ fontWeight: "bold", fontSize: "15px", color: "#111827", whiteSpace: "nowrap", textAlign: "right" }}>
                      {formatPrice(calculatedFramePrice)}
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  {/* HÃ€NG 2: THÃ”NG TIN TRÃ’NG KÃNH + GIÃ TRÃ’NG (Chá»‰ hiá»‡n khi cÃ³ chá»n trÃ²ng) */}
                  {(lensType || lensFeature) && (
                    <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", alignItems: "center", width: "100%", backgroundColor: "#f8fafc", padding: "10px 12px", borderRadius: "6px", border: "1px solid #e2e8f0" }}>
                      <div style={{ flex: 1 }}>
                        <p style={{ margin: 0, fontSize: "14px", color: "#334155", fontWeight: "500" }}>
                          TrÃ²ng kÃ­nh: {lensType || "KhÃ´ng cÃ³"}{lensFeature ? ` â€” ${lensFeature}` : ""}
                        </p>
                        {prescriptionUrl && (
                          <a href={prescriptionUrl} target="_blank" rel="noreferrer"
                            style={{ display: "inline-block", marginTop: "6px", fontSize: "13px", color: "#0284c7", fontWeight: "bold", textDecoration: "underline" }}>
                            ðŸ‘ï¸ Xem Toa thuá»‘c / ÄÆ¡n kÃ­nh
                          </a>
                        )}
                      </div>
                      {/* GIÃ TRÃ’NG KÃNH + TÃNH NÄ‚NG */}
                      <div style={{ fontWeight: "bold", fontSize: "14px", color: "#475569", whiteSpace: "nowrap", textAlign: "right" }}>
                        {totalLensPrice > 0 ? `+ ${formatPrice(totalLensPrice)}` : "Äang cáº­p nháº­t"}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  )}

                  {/* Tá»”NG TIá»€N CHO Sáº¢N PHáº¨M NÃ€Y (Bao gá»“m nhÃ¢n vá»›i sá»‘ lÆ°á»£ng) */}
                  <div style={{ textAlign: "right", marginTop: "4px", fontSize: "14px", color: "#059669", fontWeight: "bold" }}>
                    Táº¡m tÃ­nh: {formatPrice(unitPrice * qty)}
                  </div>

                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Tá»•ng cá»™ng */}
        <div style={{ textAlign: "right", fontSize: "20px", backgroundColor: "#f0fdf4", padding: "16px 20px", borderRadius: "8px", border: "1px solid #bbf7d0" }}>
          Tá»•ng cá»™ng:{" "}
          <strong style={{ color: "#111827", fontSize: "26px" }}>
            {formatPrice(order.totalAmount)}
          </strong>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState, useEffect, useContext } from "react";
import { Link, useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import { UserContext } from "../context/UserContext";
import "./OrderHistory.css";

export default function OrderHistory() {
  const { user } = useContext(UserContext);
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  const [orders, setOrders] = useState([]);
  const [preorders, setPreorders] = useState([]);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState("");
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState("all"); // "all" | "orders" | "preorders"

  // âš¡ THÃŠM HÃ€M FORMAT TIá»€N Tá»† VÃ€O ÄÃ‚Y
  const EXCHANGE_RATE = 25400;
  const formatPrice = (n) => {
    const usd = new Intl.NumberFormat("en-US", { style: "currency", currency: "USD", minimumFractionDigits: 0 }).format(n);
    const vnd = new Intl.NumberFormat("vi-VN").format(n * EXCHANGE_RATE) + " VND";
    return `${usd} (${vnd})`;
  };

  useEffect(() => {
    const token = user?.token || JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("user"))?.token;
    if (!token) {
      navigate("/login");
      return;
    }

    const fetchAll = async () => {
      setIsLoading(true);
      setError("");
      try {
        // Gá»i song song cáº£ 2 API
        const [ordersRes, preordersRes] = await Promise.all([
          fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Orders/my?page=1&pageSize=100", {
            headers: {
              "Content-Type": "application/json",
              Accept: "application/json",
              Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
            },
          }),
          fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Preorders/my", {
            headers: {
              "Content-Type": "application/json",
              Accept: "application/json",
              Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
            },
          }),
        ]);

        if (ordersRes.ok) {
          const data = await ordersRes.json();
          setOrders(data.items || data || []);
        } else if (ordersRes.status !== 404) {
          console.warn("Orders API error:", ordersRes.status);
        }

        if (preordersRes.ok) {
          const data = await preordersRes.json();
          setPreorders(data.items || data || []);
        } else if (preordersRes.status !== 404) {
          console.warn("Preorders API error:", preordersRes.status);
        }
      } catch (err) {
        setError("Lá»—i káº¿t ná»‘i. KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ táº£i lá»‹ch sá»­ Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng.");
      } finally {
        setIsLoading(false);
      }
    };

    fetchAll();
  }, [user, navigate]);

  const translateStatus = (status) => {
    const s = status?.toLowerCase();
    if (s === "pending") return { text: "Chá» xÃ¡c nháº­n", color: "#f59e0b" };
    if (s === "processing") return { text: "Äang xá»­ lÃ½", color: "#3b82f6" };
    if (s === "shipped" || s === "delivering") return { text: "Äang giao hÃ ng", color: "#8b5cf6" };
    if (s === "delivered" || s === "completed") return { text: "ThÃ nh cÃ´ng", color: "#10b981" };
    if (s === "cancelled") return { text: "ÄÃ£ huá»·", color: "#ef4444" };
    if (s === "awaiting_payment" || s === "awaitingpayment") return { text: "Chá» thanh toÃ¡n", color: "#f97316" };
    return { text: status || "KhÃ´ng rÃµ", color: "gray" };
  };

  const formatDate = (dateStr) => {
    if (!dateStr) return "â€”";
    return new Date(dateStr).toLocaleDateString("vi-VN");
  };

  // Sáº¯p xáº¿p theo ngÃ y má»›i nháº¥t
  const sortedOrders = [...orders].sort(
    (a, b) => new Date(b.orderDate || b.createdAt || 0) - new Date(a.orderDate || a.createdAt || 0)
  );
  const sortedPreorders = [...preorders].sort(
    (a, b) => new Date(b.createdAt || b.orderDate || 0) - new Date(a.createdAt || a.orderDate || 0)
  );

  const tabStyle = (tab) => ({
    padding: "10px 24px",
    borderRadius: "8px 8px 0 0",
    border: "none",
    cursor: "pointer",
    fontWeight: "bold",
    fontSize: "15px",
    backgroundColor: activeTab === tab ? "white" : "#f3f4f6",
    color: activeTab === tab ? "#111827" : "#6b7280",
    borderBottom: activeTab === tab ? "3px solid #2563eb" : "3px solid transparent",
    transition: "all 0.2s",
  });

  // Render má»™t card Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng thÆ°á»ng
  const OrderCard = ({ order }) => {
    const statusObj = translateStatus(order.status);
    const itemsList = order.orderDetails || order.orderItems || order.items || [];
    const totalQty =
      order.totalQuantity ||
      order.totalItems ||
      itemsList.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.quantity || item.qty || 1), 0);

    return (
      <div
        style={{
          marginBottom: "16px",
          border: "1px solid #e5e7eb",
          borderRadius: "10px",
          padding: "20px",
          backgroundColor: "white",
          boxShadow: "0 1px 4px rgba(0,0,0,0.05)",
        }}
      >
        <div
          style={{
            display: "flex",
            justifyContent: "space-between",
            borderBottom: "1px solid #f3f4f6",
            paddingBottom: "12px",
            marginBottom: "12px",
            flexWrap: "wrap",
            gap: "8px",
          }}
        >
          <div>
            <p style={{ margin: "0 0 4px 0", fontSize: "13px", color: "#6b7280" }}>
              <b>MÃ£ Ä‘Æ¡n:</b> #{order.id || order.orderId}
            </p>
            <p style={{ margin: 0, fontWeight: "bold", fontSize: "14px" }}>
              NgÃ y Ä‘áº·t: {formatDate(order.orderDate || order.createdAt)}
            </p>
          </div>
          <span
            style={{
              fontWeight: "bold",
              color: statusObj.color,
              backgroundColor: `${statusObj.color}18`,
              padding: "5px 14px",
              borderRadius: "20px",
              fontSize: "13px",
              alignSelf: "flex-start",
            }}
          >
            {statusObj.text}
          </span>
        </div>

        <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", alignItems: "center", flexWrap: "wrap", gap: "10px" }}>
          <div>
            <p style={{ margin: "0 0 4px 0" }}>
              Tá»•ng tiá»n:{" "}
              {/* âš¡ ÄÃƒ Sá»¬A: Gá»i hÃ m formatPrice cho Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng thÆ°á»ng */}
              <strong style={{ color: "#111827", fontSize: "18px" }}>
                {formatPrice(order.totalAmount || order.totalPrice || 0)}
              </strong>
            </p>
            <p style={{ margin: 0, fontSize: "13px", color: "#6b7280" }}>
              Sá»‘ sáº£n pháº©m: <b>{totalQty}</b>
            </p>
          </div>
          <Link
            to={`/orders/${order.id || order.orderId}`}
            style={{
              padding: "8px 18px",
              border: "1px solid #d1d5db",
              borderRadius: "6px",
              textDecoration: "none",
              color: "#111827",
              fontWeight: "500",
              fontSize: "14px",
              backgroundColor: "#f9fafb",
            }}
          >
            Xem chi tiáº¿t â†’
          </Link>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  // Render má»™t card Ä‘Æ¡n Ä‘áº·t trÆ°á»›c (PRE-ORDER)
  const PreorderCard = ({ order }) => {
    const statusObj = translateStatus(order.status);
    const itemsList = order.preorderDetails || order.items || [];
    const totalQty = itemsList.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.quantity || 1), 0);
    
    // State lÆ°u tá»•ng tiá»n Ä‘á»ƒ cÃ³ thá»ƒ update báº¥t Ä‘á»“ng bá»™
    const [finalAmount, setFinalAmount] = useState(
      order.totalAmount || order.totalPrice ||
      itemsList.reduce((sum, item) => {
        const itemPrice = item.unitPrice || item.price || 0;
        const itemQty = item.quantity || item.qty || 1;
        return sum + (itemPrice * itemQty);
      }, 0)
    );

    // âš¡ FIX: Náº¿u tá»•ng tiá»n váº«n báº±ng 0 (do BE thiáº¿u data), gá»i API Payment Ä‘á»ƒ láº¥y sá»‘ tiá»n Ä‘Ã£ tráº£
    useEffect(() => {
      const fetchPaymentAmount = async () => {
        if (finalAmount === 0 || !finalAmount) {
          try {
            const token = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("user"))?.token;
            const preId = order.id || order.preorderId;
            const res = await fetch(`https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Payments/preorder/${preId}`, {
              headers: { "Authorization": `Bearer ${token}` }
            });
            if (res.ok) {
              const data = await res.json();
              // API cÃ³ thá»ƒ tráº£ vá» 1 máº£ng cÃ¡c payment hoáº·c 1 object, ta láº¥y amount
              if (data && data.length > 0 && data[0].amount) {
                setFinalAmount(data[0].amount);
              } else if (data && data.amount) {
                setFinalAmount(data.amount);
              }
            }
          } catch (err) {
            console.error("Lá»—i láº¥y thÃ´ng tin Payment:", err);
          }
        }
      };

      fetchPaymentAmount();
    }, [order, finalAmount]);

    return (
      <div
        style={{
          marginBottom: "16px",
          border: "1px solid #bfdbfe",
          borderRadius: "10px",
          padding: "20px",
          backgroundColor: "#eff6ff",
          boxShadow: "0 1px 4px rgba(37,99,235,0.08)",
        }}
      >
        {/* Badge PRE-ORDER */}
        <div style={{ marginBottom: "10px" }}>
          <span
            style={{
              backgroundColor: "#2563eb",
              color: "white",
              fontSize: "11px",
              fontWeight: "bold",
              padding: "3px 10px",
              borderRadius: "20px",
              letterSpacing: "0.5px",
            }}
          >
            ðŸš€ PRE-ORDER
          </span>
        </div>

        <div
          style={{
            display: "flex",
            justifyContent: "space-between",
            borderBottom: "1px solid #dbeafe",
            paddingBottom: "12px",
            marginBottom: "12px",
            flexWrap: "wrap",
            gap: "8px",
          }}
        >
          <div>
            <p style={{ margin: "0 0 4px 0", fontSize: "13px", color: "#1e40af" }}>
              <b>MÃ£ Ä‘áº·t trÆ°á»›c:</b> #{order.id || order.preorderId}
            </p>
            <p style={{ margin: 0, fontWeight: "bold", fontSize: "14px", color: "#1e3a8a" }}>
              NgÃ y Ä‘áº·t: {formatDate(order.createdAt || order.orderDate)}
            </p>
            {order.expectedDate && (
              <p style={{ margin: "4px 0 0 0", fontSize: "13px", color: "#1d4ed8" }}>
                ðŸ“… Dá»± kiáº¿n giao: {formatDate(order.expectedDate)}
              </p>
            )}
          </div>
          <span
            style={{
              fontWeight: "bold",
              color: statusObj.color,
              backgroundColor: `${statusObj.color}18`,
              padding: "5px 14px",
              borderRadius: "20px",
              fontSize: "13px",
              alignSelf: "flex-start",
            }}
          >
            {statusObj.text}
          </span>
        </div>

        <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", alignItems: "center", flexWrap: "wrap", gap: "10px" }}>
          <div>
            <p style={{ margin: "0 0 4px 0" }}>
              Tá»•ng tiá»n:{" "}
              {/* âš¡ ÄÃƒ Sá»¬A: Gá»i hÃ m formatPrice cho Ä‘Æ¡n Preorder */}
              <strong style={{ color: "#1e40af", fontSize: "18px" }}>
                {formatPrice(finalAmount || 0)}
              </strong>
            </p>
            {totalQty > 0 && (
              <p style={{ margin: 0, fontSize: "13px", color: "#1e40af" }}>
                Sá»‘ sáº£n pháº©m: <b>{totalQty}</b>
              </p>
            )}
          </div>
          
         <Link 
             to={`/preorders/${order.id || order.preorderId}`}
             style={{
              padding: "8px 18px",
              border: "1px solid #93c5fd",
              borderRadius: "6px",
              textDecoration: "none",
              color: "#1e40af",
              fontWeight: "500",
              fontSize: "14px",
              backgroundColor: "white",
              cursor: "pointer",
              display: "inline-block" // GiÃºp link giá»¯ Ä‘Ãºng kÃ­ch thÆ°á»›c nÃºt
            }}
          >
            Xem chi tiáº¿t â†’
          </Link>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  };

  const totalCount = orders.length + preorders.length;

  return (
    <div style={{ maxWidth: "800px", margin: "40px auto", padding: "20px" }}>
      <h2 style={{ marginBottom: "6px" }}>Lá»‹ch Sá»­ ÄÆ¡n HÃ ng</h2>

                ))}
                {totalCount === 0 && !error && (
                  <p style={{ textAlign: "center", color: "#6b7280" }}>ChÆ°a cÃ³ Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng nÃ o.</p>
                )}
              </>
            )}

            {/* TAB: ÄÆ N THÆ¯á»œNG */}
            {activeTab === "orders" && (
              <>
                {sortedOrders.length === 0 ? (
                  <p style={{ textAlign: "center", color: "#6b7280", padding: "30px 0" }}>
                    ChÆ°a cÃ³ Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng thÆ°á»ng nÃ o.
                  </p>
                ) : (
                  sortedOrders.map((order) => (
                    <OrderCard key={order.id || order.orderId} order={order} />
                  ))
                )}
              </>
            )}

            {/* TAB: Äáº¶T TRÆ¯á»šC */}
            {activeTab === "preorders" && (
              <>
                {sortedPreorders.length === 0 ? (
                  <p style={{ textAlign: "center", color: "#6b7280", padding: "30px 0" }}>
                    ChÆ°a cÃ³ Ä‘Æ¡n Ä‘áº·t trÆ°á»›c nÃ o.
                  </p>
                ) : (
                  sortedPreorders.map((order) => (
                    <PreorderCard key={order.id || order.preorderId} order={order} />
                  ))
                )}
              </>
            )}
          </>
        )}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState, useEffect, useContext } from "react";
import { useParams, Link, useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import { UserContext } from "../context/UserContext";

export default function PreorderDetail() {
  const { id } = useParams();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { user } = useContext(UserContext);
  const [order, setOrder] = useState(null);
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState("");

  useEffect(() => {
    const token = user?.token || JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("user"))?.token;
    if (!token) { navigate("/login"); return; }

    const fetchDetail = async () => {
      try {
        const res = await fetch(`https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Preorders/${id}`, {
          headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` },
        });
        if (res.ok) {
          const data = await res.json();

          // ===== DEBUG: TÃ¬m field Ä‘á»‹a chá»‰ trong preorder response =====
          console.log("PREORDER DETAIL - Táº¤T Cáº¢ FIELDS:");
          const topLevelFields = {};
          Object.entries(data).forEach(([k, v]) => {
            if (typeof v !== "object" || v === null) topLevelFields[k] = v;
          });
          console.table(topLevelFields);
          if (data.user) {
            console.log("ðŸ‘¤ user object:", data.user);
          }
          // =============================================================

          setOrder(data);
        } else if (res.status === 404) {
          setError("KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y Ä‘Æ¡n Ä‘áº·t trÆ°á»›c nÃ y.");
        } else {
          setError(`Lá»—i ${res.status} khi táº£i chi tiáº¿t.`);
        }
      } catch {
        setError("Lá»—i káº¿t ná»‘i. Vui lÃ²ng thá»­ láº¡i.");
      } finally {
        setIsLoading(false);
      }
    };
    fetchDetail();
  }, [id, user, navigate]);

  if (isLoading)
    return <div style={{ textAlign: "center", padding: "60px", color: "#666" }}>Äang táº£i chi tiáº¿t Ä‘Æ¡n Ä‘áº·t trÆ°á»›c...</div>;

  if (error || !order)
    return (
      <div style={{ textAlign: "center", padding: "60px" }}>
        <h2 style={{ color: "#dc2626" }}>{error || "KhÃ´ng tÃ¬m tháº¥y Ä‘Æ¡n Ä‘áº·t trÆ°á»›c"}</h2>
        <Link to="/orders" style={{ color: "#3b82f6" }}>â† Quay láº¡i lá»‹ch sá»­ mua hÃ ng</Link>
      </div>
    );

  const formatUSD = (n) =>
    new Intl.NumberFormat("en-US", { style: "currency", currency: "USD", minimumFractionDigits: 0 }).format(n || 0);

  const formatDate = (d) => d ? new Date(d).toLocaleString("vi-VN") : "â€”";

  const getStatusBadge = (status) => {
    const s = status?.toLowerCase() || "";
    const map = {
      pending:          { text: "Chá» xÃ¡c nháº­n",   color: "#d97706", bg: "#fef3c7" },
      confirmed:        { text: "ÄÃ£ xÃ¡c nháº­n",    color: "#059669", bg: "#d1fae5" },
      processing:       { text: "Äang xá»­ lÃ½",     color: "#4338ca", bg: "#ede9fe" },
      awaiting_payment: { text: "Chá» thanh toÃ¡n", color: "#f97316", bg: "#fff7ed" },
      awaitingpayment:  { text: "Chá» thanh toÃ¡n", color: "#f97316", bg: "#fff7ed" },
      paid:             { text: "ÄÃ£ thanh toÃ¡n",  color: "#059669", bg: "#d1fae5" },
      shipped:          { text: "Äang giao hÃ ng", color: "#7e22ce", bg: "#f3e8ff" },
      delivered:        { text: "HoÃ n thÃ nh",     color: "#059669", bg: "#d1fae5" },
      completed:        { text: "HoÃ n thÃ nh",     color: "#059669", bg: "#d1fae5" },
      cancelled:        { text: "ÄÃ£ huá»·",         color: "#dc2626", bg: "#fee2e2" },
    };
    const s2 = map[s] || { text: status || "KhÃ´ng rÃµ", color: "#6b7280", bg: "#f3f4f6" };
    return (
      <span style={{ fontWeight: "bold", color: s2.color, backgroundColor: s2.bg, padding: "4px 14px", borderRadius: "20px", fontSize: "14px" }}>
        {s2.text}
      </span>
    );
  };

  const receiverName  = order.user?.fullName || "â€”";
  const receiverPhone = order.user?.phone    || "â€”";

  
  const shippingAddress =
    order.shippingAddress  ||
    order.deliveryAddress  ||
    order.address          ||
    order.user?.address    ||
    "â€”";

  const orderNote = order.note || "KhÃ´ng cÃ³";

  const itemsList = (order.preorderItems || order.orderItems || []).filter(Boolean);

  const totalAmount =
    order.totalAmount ||
    order.totalPrice  ||
    itemsList.reduce((sum, item) => sum + (item.orderPrice || item.preorderPrice || item.unitPrice || 0), 0);

  return (
    <div style={{ maxWidth: "860px", margin: "40px auto", padding: "20px", fontFamily: "sans-serif" }}>
      <Link to="/orders" style={{ color: "#6b7280", textDecoration: "none", fontSize: "14px", display: "inline-block", marginBottom: "20px" }}>
        â† Lá»‹ch sá»­ mua hÃ ng
      </Link>

      <div style={{ backgroundColor: "white", padding: "30px", borderRadius: "12px", boxShadow: "0 2px 12px rgba(0,0,0,0.07)" }}>

        {/* Header */}
        <div style={{ display: "flex", justifyContent: "space-between", alignItems: "flex-start", borderBottom: "2px solid #dbeafe", paddingBottom: "18px", marginBottom: "24px", flexWrap: "wrap", gap: "10px" }}>
          <div>
            <span style={{ backgroundColor: "#2563eb", color: "white", fontSize: "11px", fontWeight: "bold", padding: "3px 10px", borderRadius: "20px" }}>
              PRE-ORDER
            </span>
            <h2 style={{ margin: "8px 0 0", fontSize: "22px" }}>Chi Tiáº¿t ÄÆ¡n Äáº·t TrÆ°á»›c</h2>
            <p style={{ margin: "6px 0 0", color: "#6b7280", fontSize: "14px" }}>
              MÃ£ Ä‘Æ¡n: <b style={{ color: "#1e40af" }}>#{order.preorderId || order.id}</b>
            </p>
          </div>
          {getStatusBadge(order.status)}
        </div>

        {/* 2 cá»™t thÃ´ng tin */}
        <div style={{ display: "grid", gridTemplateColumns: "1fr 1fr", gap: "16px", marginBottom: "28px" }}>

          {/* ThÃ´ng tin Ä‘Æ¡n */}
          <div style={{ backgroundColor: "#eff6ff", padding: "18px", borderRadius: "10px", border: "1px solid #bfdbfe" }}>
            <h4 style={{ marginTop: 0, marginBottom: "12px", color: "#1e40af", fontSize: "15px", borderBottom: "1px solid #bfdbfe", paddingBottom: "8px" }}>
              ThÃ´ng tin Ä‘Æ¡n Ä‘áº·t trÆ°á»›c
            </h4>
            <p style={{ margin: "6px 0", fontSize: "14px" }}>
              <b>NgÃ y Ä‘áº·t:</b> {formatDate(order.createdAt || order.orderDate)}
            </p>
            {order.expectedDate && (

import React, { useState, useContext } from "react"; 
import { Link, useNavigate } from "react-router-dom";
import { UserContext } from "../context/UserContext"; 
import { GoogleLogin } from "@react-oauth/google"; 
import "./Auth.css";

export default function RegisterPage() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { login } = useContext(UserContext); 
  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({ fullName: "", email: "", phone: "", password: "", confirmPassword: "" });
  const [errorMsg, setErrorMsg] = useState("");
  const [successMsg, setSuccessMsg] = useState("");
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(false);

  const handleChange = (e) => setFormData(prev => ({ ...prev, [e.target.name]: e.target.value }));

  const handleRegister = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setErrorMsg(""); setSuccessMsg("");
    
    if (formData.password !== formData.confirmPassword) { 
      setErrorMsg("Máº­t kháº©u xÃ¡c nháº­n khÃ´ng khá»›p!"); 
      return; 
    }
    
    setIsLoading(true);
    try {
      const response = await fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Auth/register", {
        method: "POST", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ 
          email: formData.email, 
          password: formData.password, 
          fullName: formData.fullName, 
          phone: formData.phone 
        }),
      });
      const data = await response.json();
      
      if (response.ok || response.status === 201) {
        // âš¡ Tá»° Äá»˜NG ÄÄ‚NG NHáº¬P SAU KHI ÄÄ‚NG KÃ THÃ€NH CÃ”NG
        login({ 
          token: data.token, 
          userId: data.userId, 
          email: data.email, 
          fullName: data.fullName, 
          role: data.role 
        });
        setSuccessMsg("ÄÄƒng kÃ½ thÃ nh cÃ´ng! Äang chuyá»ƒn hÆ°á»›ng...");
        setTimeout(() => navigate("/"), 2000);
      } else { 
        setErrorMsg(data.message || "ÄÄƒng kÃ½ tháº¥t báº¡i!"); 
      }
    } catch (error) { 
      setErrorMsg("KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ káº¿t ná»‘i Ä‘áº¿n Server."); 
    } finally { 
      setIsLoading(false); 
    }
  };

  const handleGoogleSuccess = async (credentialResponse) => {
    setIsLoading(true); setErrorMsg("");
    try {
      const response = await fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Auth/google", {
        method: "POST", headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
        body: JSON.stringify({ idToken: credentialResponse.credential }),
      });
      const data = await response.json();
      if (response.ok) {
        // âš¡ ÄÄ‚NG NHáº¬P GOOGLE Tá»ª TRANG ÄÄ‚NG KÃ
        login({ 
          token: data.token, 
          userId: data.userId, 
          email: data.email, 
          fullName: data.fullName, 
          role: data.role 
        });
        navigate("/");
      } else { 
        setErrorMsg("XÃ¡c thá»±c Google tháº¥t báº¡i!"); 
      }
    } catch (error) { 
      setErrorMsg("Lá»—i káº¿t ná»‘i API Google."); 
    } finally { 
      setIsLoading(false); 
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="auth-container register-container">
      <h2 className="auth-title">ÄÄƒng KÃ½ TÃ i Khoáº£n</h2>
      
      {errorMsg && <div className="auth-msg error">{errorMsg}</div>}
      {successMsg && <div className="auth-msg success">{successMsg}</div>}

      <form onSubmit={handleRegister} className="auth-form">
        <div className="form-group">
          <label>Há» vÃ  TÃªn:</label>
          <input type="text" name="fullName" value={formData.fullName} onChange={handleChange} required placeholder="Nháº­p há» vÃ  tÃªn" />
        </div>
        <div className="form-group">
          <label>Email:</label>
          <input type="email" name="email" value={formData.email} onChange={handleChange} required placeholder="Nháº­p email" />
        </div>
        <div className="form-group">
          <label>Sá»‘ Ä‘iá»‡n thoáº¡i:</label>
          <input type="tel" name="phone" value={formData.phone} onChange={handleChange} required placeholder="Nháº­p sá»‘ Ä‘iá»‡n thoáº¡i" />
        </div>
        <div className="form-group">
          <label>Máº­t kháº©u:</label>
          <input type="password" name="password" value={formData.password} onChange={handleChange} required placeholder="Nháº­p máº­t kháº©u" />
        </div>
        <div className="form-group">
          <label>XÃ¡c nháº­n máº­t kháº©u:</label>
          <input type="password" name="confirmPassword" value={formData.confirmPassword} onChange={handleChange} required placeholder="Nháº­p láº¡i máº­t kháº©u" />
        </div>

        <button type="submit" disabled={isLoading} className="btn-submit">
          {isLoading ? "Äang xá»­ lÃ½..." : "ÄÄƒng KÃ½"}
        </button>
      </form>

      <div className="auth-divider">
        <div className="line"></div><span className="text">HOáº¶C</span><div className="line"></div>
      </div>

      <div className="auth-google-btn">
        <GoogleLogin onSuccess={handleGoogleSuccess} onError={() => setErrorMsg("ÄÄƒng kÃ½ Google tháº¥t báº¡i")} shape="pill" theme="outline" text="signup_with" />
      </div>

      <div className="auth-footer">
        ÄÃ£ cÃ³ tÃ i khoáº£n? <Link to="/login" className="auth-link">ÄÄƒng nháº­p ngay</Link>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import React, { useState, useEffect, useContext } from 'react';
import { UserContext } from '../context/UserContext';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import './UserProfile.css';

// --- 1. CÃC HÃ€M Táº O Dá»® LIá»†U DROPBOX (Äáº·t ngoÃ i Component) ---
const generateOptions = (min, max, step = 0.25) => {
  const options = [];
  for (let i = min; i <= max; i = Math.round((i + step) * 100) / 100) {
    options.push(i.toFixed(2));
  }
  return options;
};

const sphOptions = generateOptions(-20, 12, 0.25);
const cylOptions = generateOptions(-6, 6, 0.25);
const pdOptions = Array.from({ length: 79 - 57 + 1 }, (_, i) => 57 + i);
const axisOptions = Array.from({ length: 181 }, (_, i) => i);

export default function UserProfile() {
  const { user } = useContext(UserContext);
  const navigate = useNavigate();

  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState("info");
  const [profile, setProfile] = useState(null);
  const [editMode, setEditMode] = useState(false);
  const [formData, setFormData] = useState({ fullName: '', phone: '', address: '' });
  const [isLoading, setIsLoading] = useState(true);

  const [prescriptions, setPrescriptions] = useState([]);
  const [isAddingPrescription, setIsAddingPrescription] = useState(false);
  
  // State lÆ°u lá»—i theo khu vá»±c
  const [validationErrors, setValidationErrors] = useState({ right: [], left: [], other: [] });

  const [prescriptionForm, setPrescriptionForm] = useState({
    sphereRight: "0.00", cylinderRight: "0.00", axisRight: 0,
    sphereLeft: "0.00", cylinderLeft: "0.00", axisLeft: 0,
    pupillaryDistance: 60, doctorName: "", clinicName: ""
  });

  const token = user?.token || JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem("user"))?.token;

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!token) {
      navigate('/login');
      return;
    }
    fetchProfile();
    fetchPrescriptions(); 
  }, [token, navigate]);

  const fetchProfile = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Users/me", {
        headers: { "Authorization": `Bearer ${token}` }
      });
      if (res.ok) {
        const data = await res.json();
        setProfile(data);
        setFormData({ fullName: data.fullName || '', phone: data.phone || '', address: data.address || '' });
      }
    } catch (err) { console.error("Lá»—i profile"); } 
    finally { setIsLoading(false); }
  };

  const fetchPrescriptions = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Prescriptions/my?page=1&pageSize=10", {
        headers: { "Authorization": `Bearer ${token}` }
      });
      if (res.ok) {
        const data = await res.json();
        setPrescriptions(data.items || data || []);
      }
    } catch (err) { console.error("Lá»—i láº¥y toa thuá»‘c"); }
  };

  const handleUpdateProfile = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    try {
      const res = await fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Users/me", {
        method: "PUT",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", "Authorization": `Bearer ${token}` },
        body: JSON.stringify(formData)
      });
      if (res.ok) {
        alert("Cáº­p nháº­t thÃ nh cÃ´ng!");
        setEditMode(false);
        fetchProfile();
      }
    } catch (err) { alert("Lá»—i khi cáº­p nháº­t"); }
  };

  const handleSavePrescription = async (e) => {
    e.preventDefault();
    setValidationErrors({ right: [], left: [], other: [] }); 

    // KIá»‚M TRA Báº®T BUá»˜C NHáº¬P TRá»¤C (AXIS) KHI CÃ“ LOáº N (CYL) NGAY Táº I FRONTEND
    if ((Number(prescriptionForm.cylinderRight) !== 0 && Number(prescriptionForm.axisRight) === 0) || 
        (Number(prescriptionForm.cylinderLeft) !== 0 && Number(prescriptionForm.axisLeft) === 0)) {
      setValidationErrors({ other: ["Lá»—i: Khi báº¡n cÃ³ Ä‘á»™ Loáº¡n (CYL), báº¡n báº¯t buá»™c pháº£i chá»n Trá»¥c (AXIS) tá»« 1 Ä‘áº¿n 180."] });
      return;
    }
    
    // Gá»­i dá»¯ liá»‡u lÃªn Backend
    const payload = {
      SphereRight: Number(prescriptionForm.sphereRight),
      CylinderRight: Number(prescriptionForm.cylinderRight),
      AxisRight: Number(prescriptionForm.axisRight),
      AddRight: null, // Gá»­i null Ä‘á»ƒ trÃ¡nh lá»—i Range(0.75, 3.5)
      SphereLeft: Number(prescriptionForm.sphereLeft),
      CylinderLeft: Number(prescriptionForm.cylinderLeft),
      AxisLeft: Number(prescriptionForm.axisLeft),
      AddLeft: null, // Gá»­i null Ä‘á»ƒ trÃ¡nh lá»—i Range(0.75, 3.5)
      PupillaryDistance: Number(prescriptionForm.pupillaryDistance),
      DoctorName: prescriptionForm.doctorName || "KhÃ¡ch tá»± nháº­p",
      ClinicName: prescriptionForm.clinicName || "KhÃ¡ch tá»± nháº­p",
      ExpirationDate: "2026-12-31" 
    };

    try {
      const res = await fetch("https://myspectra.runasp.net/api/Prescriptions", {
        method: "POST",
        headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json", "Authorization": `Bearer ${token}` },
        body: JSON.stringify(payload)
      });
      
      if (res.ok) {
        alert("ÄÃ£ lÆ°u toa thuá»‘c thÃ nh cÃ´ng!");
        setIsAddingPrescription(false);
        fetchPrescriptions(); 
      } else {
        const err = await res.json();
        if (err.errors) {
          const allMsgs = Object.values(err.errors).flat();
          setValidationErrors({
            right: allMsgs.filter(m => m.toLowerCase().includes("right")),
            left: allMsgs.filter(m => m.toLowerCase().includes("left")),
            other: allMsgs.filter(m => !m.toLowerCase().includes("right") && !m.toLowerCase().includes("left"))
          });
        } else {
          setValidationErrors({ other: [err.message || "Lá»—i nháº­p liá»‡u. Vui lÃ²ng kiá»ƒm tra láº¡i."] });
        }
      }
    } catch (err) {
      setValidationErrors({ other: ["Lá»—i káº¿t ná»‘i máº¡ng."] });
    }
  };

  if (isLoading) return <div style={{textAlign: 'center', padding: '50px'}}>Äang táº£i...</div>;

  return (
    <div className="profile-container" style={{maxWidth: '800px', margin: '40px auto', padding: '20px', fontFamily: 'sans-serif'}}>
      <h2 style={{borderBottom: '2px solid #000', paddingBottom: '10px'}}>Quáº£n LÃ½ TÃ i Khoáº£n</h2>
      
      <div style={{display: 'flex', gap: '20px', marginBottom: '20px'}}>
        <button onClick={() => setActiveTab("info")} style={{padding: '10px 20px', fontWeight: 'bold', background: activeTab === 'info' ? '#000' : '#f3f4f6', color: activeTab === 'info' ? '#fff' : '#000', border: 'none', borderRadius: '5px', cursor: 'pointer'}}>ThÃ´ng tin cÃ¡ nhÃ¢n</button>
        <button onClick={() => setActiveTab("prescription")} style={{padding: '10px 20px', fontWeight: 'bold', background: activeTab === 'prescription' ? '#000' : '#f3f4f6', color: activeTab === 'prescription' ? '#fff' : '#000', border: 'none', borderRadius: '5px', cursor: 'pointer'}}>Toa thuá»‘c cá»§a tÃ´i</button>
      </div>

      {activeTab === "info" && (
        <div style={{background: '#f9fafb', padding: '20px', borderRadius: '8px'}}>
          {!editMode ? (
            <div>
              <p><b>Há» vÃ  tÃªn:</b> {profile?.fullName}</p>
              <p><b>Email:</b> {profile?.email}</p>
              <p><b>Sá»‘ Ä‘iá»‡n thoáº¡i:</b> {profile?.phone || 'ChÆ°a cáº­p nháº­t'}</p>
              <p><b>Äá»‹a chá»‰:</b> {profile?.address || 'ChÆ°a cáº­p nháº­t'}</p>
              <button onClick={() => setEditMode(true)} style={{marginTop: '15px', padding: '10px 20px', background: '#3b82f6', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: '5px', cursor: 'pointer'}}>Sá»­a ThÃ´ng Tin</button>
            </div>
          ) : (
            <form onSubmit={handleUpdateProfile} style={{display: 'flex', flexDirection: 'column', gap: '15px'}}>
              <input type="text" value={formData.fullName} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, fullName: e.target.value})} placeholder="Há» vÃ  tÃªn" required style={{padding: '10px'}} />
              <input type="text" value={formData.phone} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, phone: e.target.value})} placeholder="Sá»‘ Ä‘iá»‡n thoáº¡i" required style={{padding: '10px'}} />
              <input type="text" value={formData.address} onChange={e => setFormData({...formData, address: e.target.value})} placeholder="Äá»‹a chá»‰ giao hÃ ng" required style={{padding: '10px'}} />
              <div style={{display: 'flex', gap: '10px'}}>
                <button type="submit" style={{padding: '10px 20px', background: '#10b981', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: '5px', cursor: 'pointer'}}>LÆ°u thay Ä‘á»•i</button>
                <button type="button" onClick={() => setEditMode(false)} style={{padding: '10px 20px', background: '#ef4444', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: '5px', cursor: 'pointer'}}>Há»§y</button>
              </div>
            </form>
          )}
        </div>
      )}

      {activeTab === "prescription" && (
        <div style={{background: '#f9fafb', padding: '20px', borderRadius: '8px'}}>
          
          {!isAddingPrescription ? (
            <>
              <button onClick={() => { setIsAddingPrescription(true); setValidationErrors({right:[], left:[], other:[]}); }} style={{padding: '10px 20px', background: '#111827', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: '5px', cursor: 'pointer', marginBottom: '20px'}}>+ ThÃªm toa Ä‘o máº¯t má»›i</button>
              
              {prescriptions.length === 0 ? <p>Báº¡n chÆ°a lÆ°u toa thuá»‘c nÃ o.</p> : (
                prescriptions.map((p, idx) => (
                  <div key={idx} style={{background: 'white', padding: '15px', borderRadius: '8px', border: '1px solid #e5e7eb', marginBottom: '15px', position: 'relative'}}>
                    {p.isExpired && <span style={{position: 'absolute', top: '10px', right: '10px', background: '#fee2e2', color: '#b91c1c', padding: '3px 8px', borderRadius: '4px', fontSize: '12px', fontWeight: 'bold'}}>ÄÃ£ háº¿t háº¡n</span>}
                    <h4 style={{marginTop: 0, color: '#4338ca'}}>Toa thuá»‘c {new Date(p.createdAt).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')}</h4>
                    <p style={{margin: '5px 0', fontSize: '14px'}}><b>BÃ¡c sÄ©/PhÃ²ng khÃ¡m:</b> {p.doctorName} - {p.clinicName}</p>
                    <p style={{margin: '5px 0', fontSize: '14px'}}><b>NgÃ y háº¿t háº¡n:</b> {new Date(p.expirationDate).toLocaleDateString('vi-VN')}</p>
                    
                    <div style={{display: 'flex', gap: '20px', marginTop: '15px', padding: '10px', background: '#f3f4f6', borderRadius: '6px'}}>
                      <div>
                        <strong style={{color: '#dc2626'}}>Máº¯t Pháº£i (R):</strong>
                        <div style={{fontSize: '14px'}}>Cáº­n/Viá»…n (SPH): {p.sphereRight} | Loáº¡n (CYL): {p.cylinderRight} | Trá»¥c (AXIS): {p.axisRight}</div>
                      </div>
                      <div style={{borderLeft: '1px solid #ccc', paddingLeft: '20px'}}>
                        <strong style={{color: '#2563eb'}}>Máº¯t TrÃ¡i (L):</strong>
                        <div style={{fontSize: '14px'}}>Cáº­n/Viá»…n (SPH): {p.sphereLeft} | Loáº¡n (CYL): {p.cylinderLeft} | Trá»¥c (AXIS): {p.axisLeft}</div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                    <p style={{margin: '10px 0 0 0', fontWeight: 'bold'}}>Khoáº£ng cÃ¡ch Ä‘á»“ng tá»­ (PD): {p.pupillaryDistance} mm</p>
                  </div>
                ))
              )}
            </>
          ) : (
            <form onSubmit={handleSavePrescription} style={{background: 'white', padding: '20px', borderRadius: '8px', border: '1px solid #e5e7eb'}}>
              <h3 style={{marginTop: 0}}>ThÃªm Toa Thuá»‘c Má»›i</h3>
              <p style={{fontSize: '13px', color: '#666', marginBottom: '20px'}}>Vui lÃ²ng Ä‘iá»n cÃ¡c thÃ´ng sá»‘ theo giáº¥y khÃ¡m máº¯t cá»§a báº¡n. (Sá»‘ Ã¢m lÃ  cáº­n, sá»‘ dÆ°Æ¡ng lÃ  viá»…n).</p>
              
              <div style={{display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: '1fr 1fr', gap: '20px'}}>
                
                {/* --- Máº®T PHáº¢I (OD) --- */}
                <div style={{border: '1px solid #fca5a5', padding: '15px', borderRadius: '6px', backgroundColor: '#fff5f5'}}>
                  <h4 style={{color: '#dc2626', marginTop: 0}}>Máº¯t Pháº£i (OD/Right)</h4>
                  
                  <label style={{display: 'block', fontSize: '13px', marginBottom: '5px', fontWeight: 'bold'}}>Äá»™ Cáº§u (SPH):</label>
                  <select 
                    style={{width: '100%', padding: '8px', marginBottom: '10px', borderRadius: '4px', border: '1px solid #ccc'}}
                    value={prescriptionForm.sphereRight}
                    onChange={e => setPrescriptionForm({...prescriptionForm, sphereRight: e.target.value})}
                  >
                    {sphOptions.map(v => <option key={v} value={v}>{v > 0 ? `+${v}` : v}</option>)}
                  </select>
                  
                  <label style={{display: 'block', fontSize: '13px', marginBottom: '5px', fontWeight: 'bold'}}>Äá»™ Loáº¡n (CYL):</label>
                  <select 
                    style={{width: '100%', padding: '8px', marginBottom: '10px', borderRadius: '4px', border: '1px solid #ccc'}}
                    value={prescriptionForm.cylinderRight}
                    onChange={e => {
                      const val = e.target.value;
                      let newAxis = prescriptionForm.axisRight;
                      
                      if (Number(val) === 0) {
                        newAxis = 0; // Náº¿u háº¿t loáº¡n thÃ¬ tráº£ Trá»¥c vá» 0
                      } else if (Number(newAxis) === 0) {
                        newAxis = 1; // Äá»“ng bá»™ UI nháº£y sá»‘ 1 thÃ¬ state cÅ©ng lÃ  1
                      }
                  
                      setPrescriptionForm({ 
                        ...prescriptionForm, 
                        cylinderRight: val, 
                        axisRight: newAxis 
                      });
                    }}
                  >
                    {cylOptions.map(v => <option key={v} value={v}>{v > 0 ? `+${v}` : v}</option>)}
                  </select>
                  
                  <label style={{display: 'block', fontSize: '13px', marginBottom: '5px', fontWeight: 'bold', color: Number(prescriptionForm.cylinderRight) === 0 ? '#aaa' : '#000'}}>Trá»¥c (AXIS) 0-180:</label>
                  <select 
                    disabled={Number(prescriptionForm.cylinderRight) === 0}
                    style={{
                      width: '100%', padding: '8px', borderRadius: '4px', border: '1px solid #ccc',
                      backgroundColor: Number(prescriptionForm.cylinderRight) === 0 ? '#f3f4f6' : '#fff'
                    }}
                    value={prescriptionForm.axisRight}
                    onChange={e => setPrescriptionForm({...prescriptionForm, axisRight: e.target.value})}
                  >
                    {axisOptions.map(v => (Number(prescriptionForm.cylinderRight) !== 0 && v === 0) ? null : <option key={v} value={v}>{v}</option>)}
                  </select>

                  {/* Hiá»‡n lá»—i Máº¯t Pháº£i */}
                  {validationErrors.right?.length > 0 && (
                    <ul style={{ margin: '10px 0 0 0', paddingLeft: '15px', color: '#be123c', fontSize: '12px', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>
                      {validationErrors.right.map((err, i) => <li key={i}>{err}</li>)}
                    </ul>
                  )}
                </div>

                {/* --- Máº®T TRÃI (OS) --- */}
                <div style={{border: '1px solid #93c5fd', padding: '15px', borderRadius: '6px', backgroundColor: '#eff6ff'}}>
                  <h4 style={{color: '#2563eb', marginTop: 0}}>Máº¯t TrÃ¡i (OS/Left)</h4>
                  
                  <label style={{display: 'block', fontSize: '13px', marginBottom: '5px', fontWeight: 'bold'}}>Äá»™ Cáº§u (SPH):</label>
                  <select 
                    style={{width: '100%', padding: '8px', marginBottom: '10px', borderRadius: '4px', border: '1px solid #ccc'}}
                    value={prescriptionForm.sphereLeft}
                    onChange={e => setPrescriptionForm({...prescriptionForm, sphereLeft: e.target.value})}
                  >
                    {sphOptions.map(v => <option key={v} value={v}>{v > 0 ? `+${v}` : v}</option>)}
                  </select>
                  
                  <label style={{display: 'block', fontSize: '13px', marginBottom: '5px', fontWeight: 'bold'}}>Äá»™ Loáº¡n (CYL):</label>
                  <select 
                    style={{width: '100%', padding: '8px', marginBottom: '10px', borderRadius: '4px', border: '1px solid #ccc'}}
                    value={prescriptionForm.cylinderLeft}
                    onChange={e => {
                      const val = e.target.value;
                      let newAxis = prescriptionForm.axisLeft;
                      
                      if (Number(val) === 0) {
                        newAxis = 0; 
                      } else if (Number(newAxis) === 0) {
                        newAxis = 1; 
                      }
                  
                      setPrescriptionForm({ 
                        ...prescriptionForm, 
                        cylinderLeft: val, 
                        axisLeft: newAxis 
                      });
                    }}
                  >
                    {cylOptions.map(v => <option key={v} value={v}>{v > 0 ? `+${v}` : v}</option>)}
                  </select>
                  
                  <label style={{display: 'block', fontSize: '13px', marginBottom: '5px', fontWeight: 'bold', color: Number(prescriptionForm.cylinderLeft) === 0 ? '#aaa' : '#000'}}>Trá»¥c (AXIS) 0-180:</label>
                  <select 
                    disabled={Number(prescriptionForm.cylinderLeft) === 0}
                    style={{
                      width: '100%', padding: '8px', borderRadius: '4px', border: '1px solid #ccc',
                      backgroundColor: Number(prescriptionForm.cylinderLeft) === 0 ? '#f3f4f6' : '#fff'
                    }}
                    value={prescriptionForm.axisLeft}
                    onChange={e => setPrescriptionForm({...prescriptionForm, axisLeft: e.target.value})}
                  >
                    {axisOptions.map(v => (Number(prescriptionForm.cylinderLeft) !== 0 && v === 0) ? null : <option key={v} value={v}>{v}</option>)}
                  </select>

                  {/* Hiá»‡n lá»—i Máº¯t TrÃ¡i */}
                  {validationErrors.left?.length > 0 && (
                    <ul style={{ margin: '10px 0 0 0', paddingLeft: '15px', color: '#be123c', fontSize: '12px', fontWeight: 'bold' }}>
                      {validationErrors.left.map((err, i) => <li key={i}>{err}</li>)}
                    </ul>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* --- PD VÃ€ BÃC SÄ¨ --- */}
              <div style={{marginTop: '20px', padding: '15px', backgroundColor: '#f9fafb', borderRadius: '8px'}}>
                <label style={{fontWeight: 'bold', display: 'inline-block', marginBottom: '5px'}}>Khoáº£ng cÃ¡ch Ä‘á»“ng tá»­ (PD - mm):</label>
                <select 
                  style={{marginLeft: '10px', padding: '8px', borderRadius: '4px', border: '1px solid #ccc', fontWeight: 'bold'}}
                  value={prescriptionForm.pupillaryDistance}
                  onChange={e => setPrescriptionForm({...prescriptionForm, pupillaryDistance: e.target.value})}
                >
                  {pdOptions.map(v => <option key={v} value={v}>{v}</option>)}
                </select>
              </div>

              <div style={{display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: '1fr 1fr', gap: '20px', marginTop: '20px'}}>
                <div>
                  <label style={{display: 'block', fontSize: '13px', marginBottom: '5px', fontWeight: 'bold'}}>TÃªn BÃ¡c sÄ© (TÃ¹y chá»n):</label>
                  <input type="text" value={prescriptionForm.doctorName} onChange={e => setPrescriptionForm({...prescriptionForm, doctorName: e.target.value})} style={{width: '100%', padding: '10px', borderRadius: '4px', border: '1px solid #ccc'}} placeholder="Nháº­p tÃªn bÃ¡c sÄ©..." />
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label style={{display: 'block', fontSize: '13px', marginBottom: '5px', fontWeight: 'bold'}}>PhÃ²ng khÃ¡m/Bá»‡nh viá»‡n (TÃ¹y chá»n):</label>
                  <input type="text" value={prescriptionForm.clinicName} onChange={e => setPrescriptionForm({...prescriptionForm, clinicName: e.target.value})} style={{width: '100%', padding: '10px', borderRadius: '4px', border: '1px solid #ccc'}} placeholder="Nháº­p tÃªn phÃ²ng khÃ¡m..." />
                </div>
              </div>

              {/* Lá»—i KhÃ¡c */}
              {validationErrors.other?.length > 0 && (
                <div style={{ marginTop: '15px', padding: '10px', backgroundColor: '#fff1f2', color: '#be123c', borderRadius: '6px', fontSize: '13px', fontWeight: 'bold', textAlign: 'center' }}>
                  âš ï¸ {validationErrors.other.join(" | ")}
                </div>
              )}

              <div style={{display: 'flex', gap: '10px', marginTop: '25px'}}>
                <button type="submit" style={{padding: '12px 25px', background: '#10b981', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: '6px', cursor: 'pointer', fontWeight: 'bold', fontSize: '15px'}}>LÆ°u Toa Thuá»‘c</button>
                <button type="button" onClick={() => setIsAddingPrescription(false)} style={{padding: '12px 25px', background: '#ef4444', color: 'white', border: 'none', borderRadius: '6px', cursor: 'pointer', fontWeight: 'bold', fontSize: '15px'}}>Há»§y bá»</button>
              </div>
            </form>
          )}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
