import React, { useEffect, useState } from "react";
import { useSearchParams, Link } from "react-router-dom";

export default function VNPayReturnPage() {
  const [searchParams] = useSearchParams();
  const [status, setStatus] = useState("loading");

  // CÃ¡c params cÃ³ thá»ƒ nháº­n Ä‘Æ°á»£c tá»« VNPay hoáº·c Backend cá»§a báº¡n
  const responseCode = searchParams.get("vnp_ResponseCode");
  const transactionNo = searchParams.get("vnp_TransactionNo") || searchParams.get("transactionId");
  const amount = searchParams.get("vnp_Amount") || searchParams.get("amount");
  const message = searchParams.get("message");
  const paymentId = searchParams.get("paymentId");
  
  // ThÃªm dÃ²ng nÃ y Ä‘á»ƒ báº¯t tham sá»‘ success tá»« URL cá»§a báº¡n
  const successParam = searchParams.get("success"); 

  useEffect(() => {
    // Debug: in ra params Ä‘á»ƒ kiá»ƒm tra
    console.log("ðŸ”µ VNPay Return Params:", {
      responseCode,
      transactionNo,
      amount,
      message,
      paymentId,
      successParam,
      fullUrl: window.location.search,
    });

    // Æ¯u tiÃªn 1: Kiá»ƒm tra theo chuáº©n VNPay gá»‘c
    if (responseCode === "00") {
      setStatus("success");
    } else if (responseCode) {
      setStatus("failed");
    } 
    // Æ¯u tiÃªn 2: Kiá»ƒm tra theo tham sá»‘ "success" tá»« Backend custom cá»§a báº¡n
    else if (successParam !== null) {
      setStatus(successParam === "true" ? "success" : "failed");
    } 
    // Æ¯u tiÃªn 3: Kiá»ƒm tra theo message (náº¿u cÃ³)
    else if (message) {
      const isSuccess =
        message.toLowerCase().includes("success") ||
        message.toLowerCase().includes("thÃ nh cÃ´ng");
      setStatus(isSuccess ? "success" : "failed");
    } 
    // Náº¿u khÃ´ng cÃ³ báº¥t ká»³ param nÃ o há»£p lá»‡
    else {
      setStatus("failed");
    }
  }, [responseCode, message, successParam]);

  const formatAmount = (raw) => {
    if (!raw) return "â€”";
    
    const EXCHANGE_RATE = 25400; 
    let amountUSD = 0;
    let amountVND = 0;
    let rawNumber = Number(raw);

    // 1. TrÆ°á»ng há»£p Backend tráº£ vá» tháº³ng tiá»n USD (VÃ­ dá»¥: 180)
    // CÃ¡c Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng thÆ°á»ng nhá» hÆ¡n 10.000 USD nÃªn dÃ¹ng má»‘c nÃ y Ä‘á»ƒ nháº­n diá»‡n
    if (rawNumber < 10000) {
      amountUSD = rawNumber; // Kháº³ng Ä‘á»‹nh Ä‘Ã¢y lÃ  180 USD
      amountVND = amountUSD * EXCHANGE_RATE; // 180 * 26250 = 4.725.000 VND
    } 
    // 2. TrÆ°á»ng há»£p tráº£ vá» chuáº©n vnp_Amount cá»§a VNPay (Tiá»n VND nhÃ¢n 100)
    // VÃ­ dá»¥: 472500000
    else if (rawNumber > 1000000) {
      amountVND = rawNumber / 100; // 472500000 / 100 = 4.725.000 VND
      amountUSD = amountVND / EXCHANGE_RATE; 
    } 
    // 3. TrÆ°á»ng há»£p tráº£ vá» tiá»n VND bÃ¬nh thÆ°á»ng (VÃ­ dá»¥: 4725000)
    else {
      amountVND = rawNumber;
      amountUSD = amountVND / EXCHANGE_RATE;
    }

    // Äá»‹nh dáº¡ng USD (vÃ­ dá»¥: $180)
    const formattedUSD = new Intl.NumberFormat("en-US", {
      style: "currency",
      currency: "USD",
      minimumFractionDigits: 0
    }).format(amountUSD);

    // Äá»‹nh dáº¡ng VND (vÃ­ dá»¥: 4.725.000 VND)
    const formattedVND = new Intl.NumberFormat("vi-VN").format(amountVND) + " VND";

    // Tráº£ vá» chuá»—i ghÃ©p: $180 (4.725.000 VND)
    return `${formattedUSD} (${formattedVND})`;
  };

  return (
    <div
      style={{
        textAlign: "center",
        padding: "80px 20px",
        fontFamily: "sans-serif",
        minHeight: "60vh",
        display: "flex",
        alignItems: "center",
        justifyContent: "center",
      }}
    >
      {/* LOADING */}
      {status === "loading" && (
        <div>
          <div style={{ fontSize: "50px", marginBottom: "16px" }}>â³</div>
          <h2 style={{ color: "#6b7280" }}>Äang kiá»ƒm tra káº¿t quáº£ thanh toÃ¡n...</h2>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* THÃ€NH CÃ”NG */}
      {status === "success" && (
        <div
          style={{
            backgroundColor: "#f0fdf4",
            maxWidth: "500px",
            width: "100%",
            margin: "0 auto",
            padding: "40px 30px",
            borderRadius: "16px",
            border: "1px solid #bbf7d0",
            boxShadow: "0 4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.08)",
          }}
        >
          <div style={{ fontSize: "64px" }}>âœ…</div>
          <h2 style={{ color: "#059669", marginTop: "12px", fontSize: "24px" }}>
            Thanh ToÃ¡n VNPay ThÃ nh CÃ´ng!
          </h2>
          <p style={{ color: "#374151", marginTop: "8px" }}>
            Cáº£m Æ¡n báº¡n! ÄÆ¡n hÃ ng cá»§a báº¡n Ä‘Ã£ Ä‘Æ°á»£c ghi nháº­n.
          </p>

          <div
            style={{
              textAlign: "left",
              backgroundColor: "white",
              padding: "16px",
              borderRadius: "10px",
              marginTop: "20px",
              border: "1px solid #d1fae5",
            }}
          >
            {transactionNo && (
              <p style={{ margin: "6px 0", color: "#374151", fontSize: "14px" }}>
                <b>MÃ£ giao dá»‹ch:</b> {transactionNo}
              </p>
            )}
            {paymentId && (
              <p style={{ margin: "6px 0", color: "#374151", fontSize: "14px" }}>
                <b>Payment ID:</b> {paymentId}
              </p>
            )}
            {amount && (
              <p style={{ margin: "6px 0", color: "#374151", fontSize: "14px" }}>
                <b>Sá»‘ tiá»n:</b> {formatAmount(amount)}
              </p>
            )}
          </div>

          <div
            style={{ display: "flex", gap: "12px", marginTop: "24px", justifyContent: "center" }}
          >
            <Link
              to="/orders"
              style={{
                display: "inline-block",
                padding: "12px 24px",
                backgroundColor: "#059669",
                color: "white",
                textDecoration: "none",
                borderRadius: "8px",
                fontWeight: "bold",
                fontSize: "15px",
              }}
            >
              Xem Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng
            </Link>
            <Link
              to="/"
              style={{
                display: "inline-block",
                padding: "12px 24px",
                backgroundColor: "#111827",
                color: "white",
                textDecoration: "none",
                borderRadius: "8px",
                fontWeight: "bold",
                fontSize: "15px",
              }}
            >
              Vá» trang chá»§
            </Link>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* THáº¤T Báº I */}
      {status === "failed" && (
        <div
          style={{
            backgroundColor: "#fef2f2",
            maxWidth: "500px",
            width: "100%",
            margin: "0 auto",
            padding: "40px 30px",
            borderRadius: "16px",
            border: "1px solid #fecaca",
            boxShadow: "0 4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,0.08)",
          }}
        >
          <div style={{ fontSize: "64px" }}>âŒ</div>
          <h2 style={{ color: "#dc2626", marginTop: "12px", fontSize: "24px" }}>
            Thanh ToÃ¡n Tháº¥t Báº¡i
          </h2>
          <p style={{ color: "#374151", marginTop: "8px" }}>
            Giao dá»‹ch chÆ°a Ä‘Æ°á»£c hoÃ n táº¥t. ÄÆ¡n hÃ ng váº«n Ä‘Æ°á»£c lÆ°u â€” báº¡n cÃ³ thá»ƒ thá»­ thanh toÃ¡n láº¡i.
          </p>

          {/* Hiá»ƒn thá»‹ lÃ½ do tháº¥t báº¡i náº¿u cÃ³ */}
          {(responseCode || message) && (
            <div
              style={{
                textAlign: "left",
                backgroundColor: "white",
                padding: "12px 16px",
                borderRadius: "8px",
                marginTop: "16px",
                border: "1px solid #fecaca",
              }}
            >
              {responseCode && responseCode !== "00" && (
                <p style={{ margin: "4px 0", fontSize: "13px", color: "#6b7280" }}>
                  <b>MÃ£ lá»—i VNPay:</b> {responseCode}
                </p>
              )}
              {message && (
                <p style={{ margin: "4px 0", fontSize: "13px", color: "#6b7280" }}>
                  <b>Chi tiáº¿t:</b> {decodeURIComponent(message)}
                </p>
              )}
            </div>
          )}

          <div
            style={{ display: "flex", gap: "12px", marginTop: "24px", justifyContent: "center" }}
          >
            <Link
              to="/orders"
              style={{
                display: "inline-block",
                padding: "12px 24px",
                backgroundColor: "#dc2626",
                color: "white",
                textDecoration: "none",
                borderRadius: "8px",
                fontWeight: "bold",
                fontSize: "15px",
              }}
            >
              Xem Ä‘Æ¡n hÃ ng
            </Link>
            <Link
              to="/"
              style={{
                display: "inline-block",
                padding: "12px 24px",
                backgroundColor: "#6b7280",
                color: "white",
                textDecoration: "none",
                borderRadius: "8px",
                fontWeight: "bold",
                fontSize: "15px",
              }}
            >
              Vá» trang chá»§
            </Link>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}



========================================
FILE: routes\AdminProtectedRoute.jsx
========================================

import React, { useContext } from 'react';
import { Navigate, Outlet } from 'react-router-dom';
import { UserContext } from '../context/UserContext';

export default function AdminProtectedRoute() {
  const { user } = useContext(UserContext);

  // Láº¥y role tá»« user context (chuáº©n chá»¯ thÆ°á»ng)
  const role = user?.role || "";

  // Cho phÃ©p admin, manager vÃ  staff vÃ o khu vá»±c quáº£n trá»‹ chung.
  if (role !== "admin" && role !== "manager" && role !== "staff") {
    return <Navigate to="/" replace />;
  }
  
  return <Outlet />;
}

// --- IMPORT CÃC COMPONENT LAYOUT ---

  return (

          <Route path="/register" element={<RegisterPage />} />
          <Route path="/profile" element={<UserProfile />} />
        </Route>

      </Routes>
    </Router>

}

import React from "react";
import AppRouter from "./routes/AppRouter";
import { CartProvider } from "./context/CartContext";
import { OrderProvider } from "./context/OrderContext"; 
import { UserProvider } from "./context/UserContext"; 

function App() {
  return (
    <UserProvider>  
      <OrderProvider>
        <CartProvider>
          <AppRouter />
        </CartProvider>
      </OrderProvider>
    </UserProvider>
  );
}

export default App;
